{~f120v~}\n
{=The text begins immediately below the end of the Ancrene Riwle in Hand\n
A, and slightly less than half way down the folio. The first letter of\n
each verse line is placed in a separately ruled column. Although these\n
are only occasional majuscule in shape, I take the separation to\n
distinguish them as litterae notabiliores and I have therefore\n
designated them as capitals with preceding asterisks=}\n
{\'}\n
